***keutel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:keutel.html>keutel</a> (104443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cotel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cuetel</i>. Probably a derivative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">koot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus originally “something hard”. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Köttel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keutel.html>keutel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keutel.html>keutels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keutel.html>keuteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a small piece of hard (chiefly animal) feces</li></ol>

***keuvelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:keuvelen.html>keuvelen</a> (60434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kevel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>. The -eu- arose due to spontaneous rounding in Hollandic dialects. 
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kever.html>kever</a> (14130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kever.html>kever</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kevero</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*kefrō</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chafer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Käfer</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kiek.html>kiek</a> (104436)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the name of Dutch photographer Israël <a href = vnd.unilang:kiek.html>Kiek</a>. Probably reinforced by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kijk.html>kijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a></i>, a dialectal synonym for <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiek.html>kiek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiekje.html>kiekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A snapshot, photograph; orinally specifically used for a group scene and/or shot by an amateur photographer</li></ol>

***kieken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a> (104435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kiukīną</i>, cognate with chicken. Doublet with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kiekens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kiekentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chick, young domestic fowl
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dumb bird, derogatory term for a (usually female) airhead

***kiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kiel.html>kiel</a> (20770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiel.html>kiel</a></i>, probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kjǫlr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*keluz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiel.html>kiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiel.html>kielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiel.html>kieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bottom side of a ship: the <a href = vnd.unilang:keel.html>keel</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***kiem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kiem.html>kiem</a> (28130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiemen.html>kieme</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kyme</i>. Although the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found as Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kīmo</i>, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">kīme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">kīmo</i> because it <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not undergo the regular change of <i>-ī-</i> to <i>-ij-</i> (so that <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*kijm</i> would be expected). Possible influence of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cyma</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also possible. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kīmô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiem.html>kiem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiemen.html>kiemen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiem.html>kiempje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> seed, sprout, germ</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beginning, birth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> germ (pathogen)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> germ</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kiesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kiesan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*keusaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵews-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to choose</li></ol>

<p>An onomatopoeia for the frog's sound. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kikken.html>kikken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kil.html>kil</a> (13178)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kille.html>kille</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Köle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kühl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">køle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:kyla.html>kyla</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">kylur</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chill</i>. 
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kil.html>kil</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">killer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kilst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cold-hearted, cold-blooded</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of temperatures, weather, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> cold, chilly</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kille.html>kille</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*killa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kiljǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kil.html>kil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:killen.html>killen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kil.html>killetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">creek</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rivulet</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***kiloton.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kiloton.html>kiloton</a> (49174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>metric prefix <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kilo-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ton</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiloton.html>kiloton</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kilotons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A measure of the strength of an explosion or a bomb based on how many thousand tons of TNT would be needed to produce the same energy.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That's a 300-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:kiloton.html>kiloton</a></b> nuclear warhead.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:megaton.html>megaton</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gigaton</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kiloton.html>kiloton</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li>1000 ton</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kinne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kinni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kinnuz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵénus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***kind.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> (317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kint</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kint</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kindą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">offspring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵenh₁tóm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> produced, that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> given birth to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵn̥h₁tós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">produced, given birth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵenh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to produce, to give birth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinders.html>kinders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kindje.html>kindje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindertje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindeken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindelijn</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>child, kid, non-adult human
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieve.html>Lieve</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">typical paedagogical window message during COVID-19 measures</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dear <b>children</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> miss you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>descendant, still a minor or irrespective of age
<dl><dd><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:patriarchale.html>patriarchale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tradities.html>tradities</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:levenslang.html>levenslang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onvoorwaardelijk.html>onvoorwaardelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderworpen.html>onderworpen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaderlijk.html>vaderlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezag.html>gezag</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanvankelijk.html>aanvankelijk</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>Oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houdt.html>houdt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezin.html>gezin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stichten.html>stichten</a></i>
<dl><dd>In certain patriarchal traditions, children remain subject to unconditional paternal authority for life, as originally in Ancient <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a>, in other <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> a son ceases to be a child by founding his own family</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstammeling.html>afstammeling</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:telg.html>telg</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> product of influence, breeding etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></i>. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kinders.html>kinders</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> colloquially.</li>
<li>In compounds, the word can take the form <i>kinder-</i> or <i>kind-</i>. The former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used more often, however.</li>
<li>The dimunitive <i>kindelijn</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now archaic, but can still be found in some fossilized <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> and religious texts.</li></ul>

</p>
